Roosevelt Declares War on Arms Dealers, Forms Committee to Control Arms Trade

Drafting a Plan Similar to Wartime Regulations

Eliminating Profiteering and Guaranteeing Equal Distribution

(Washington) The United States government has begun to declare war on arms dealers. President Roosevelt convened subordinates today to organize a powerful general staff to implement opposition to arms dealers who profit from murder. Within hours of the President's declaration of war, the department held a meeting to begin drafting a mobilization plan. This plan is similar to the War Department's wartime mobilization regulations, meaning that the capital of arms dealers should be controlled by the government during wartime, and the price of arms should be regulated. The President's sudden move was the result of the Senate Arms Investigation Committee's discovery of various facts about the international activities of arms dealers. In addition to all cabinet members, the new staff currently being organized includes 15 prominent leaders from various sectors of the national economy, politics, finance, commerce, and labor. Senate Arms Investigation Committee Chairman Nye believes that the President's move is a bit premature. The White House intends to limit the arms industry, while DuPont CEO DuPont Eglini said that the President's proposal is very good. However, other than that, Mr. DuPont did not show any sign of satisfaction. President Roosevelt said that the plan drafted at this meeting should take into account human issues. During the European War, the mobilization was not equal, so frontline soldiers only received one dollar a day, while workers manufacturing arms lived comfortably in the United States and could earn eight to ten dollars a day. The current demand of veterans for immediate payment of pensions is also the result of this relationship. Mr. Roosevelt also said that his actions were not due to any international crisis, but only to consider what the United States should do in case of war. It is more appropriate to implement this kind of law only when there is no danger of war at present. However, in any case, this move is not a preparation for war. The President believes that this meeting can agree on a thorough plan, which he can submit in a special message after Congress opens. He also indicated that this plan will be one of the most important bills in the next Congress. Mr. Roosevelt further indicated that the scope of the discussion at the meeting will be very broad, not only from the perspective of the interests of arms dealers, but also from an economic point of view, and pay attention to the lessons learned from the European War. In addition to the cabinet members, attendees at the first meeting included former NRA Director General Johnson, US Army Chief of Staff McCard, Federal Railway Adjustment Director Eastman, President's International Trade Advisor Pick, prominent banker and economist Baruch, Undersecretary of the Navy Henry Roosevelt, Undersecretary of Agriculture Brain Trust Leader Tugwell, and Undersecretary of Labor McGrady. The government has always appointed committees, but never before have so many well-known figures gathered together. Therefore, the President's emphasis on this matter can be seen. The strangest thing is that none of the people in the Senate Investigation Committee expressed enthusiasm for this. Senator Vandenberg, a member of the Investigation Committee, said that he did not welcome this kind of cooperation, but he also knew that Congress was very willing to handle this matter itself. Chairman Nye, in addition to complaining that the timing was not ripe, also said that the various departments of the government were actually co-defendants with the arms dealers. The new committee will be named the "War Profits Committee." Mr. Baruch was elected as chairman. Mr. Baruch declared that limiting the activities of arms dealers by levying excessive profit tax is the most effective method. Mr. Baruch praised the Senate Investigation Committee very much, and said that there was no conflict between the two sides. It is learned that the plan drafted by the new committee is quite similar to the War Department's wartime regulations, including the following: (1) Organize an industrial control bureau, similar to the industrial bureau during the European War; (2) Guarantee equal distribution of labor; (4) Preserve the capital of the arms industry; (5) Establish special trade agencies to control the international trade of the arms industry. (National Telegram, 12th)

The Truth About Arms Manufacturing in Various Countries

British Vickers Factory Makes Huge Profits

Chamberlain and Simon are Both Major Shareholders

Zaharoff Became Rich by Selling Arms

Destroying Peace and Ruining Civilization

▲National Society Indian Calcutta Correspondence American submarine building office's electric boat company officials, in the Senate investigation committee announced that the American arms factory Vickers Armstrong and the American submarine building office electric boat company have signed a contract, all of which cannot be described in detail in a few words. The officials frankly admitted that they had paid commissions for South American business, and when the investigation began, they declared that the American company had paid Sir Zaharoff, a great financier, 150,000 pounds sterling between 1919 and 1930 as a kickback for receiving an order from the Spanish government in the United States to purchase submarines. This statement did not attract any attention at the time. But then who is Zaharoff? A few years ago, a poor Greek man named Zacharias came to England, that is, today's Sir Zaharoff, suddenly the largest arms dealer in the history of the world. Mr. Qi first made a profit from running dogs in the Balkans and the Near East. The South African War arose in response, and at that time he was quite close to Lloyd George. At that time, his private property was no less than one trillion gold yuan. Mr. Qi is now eighty years old, but his twilight years are still not enough to prevent him from making huge profits by manufacturing ordnance. The director of the American Electric Boat Company, Mr. Qi, is one of the greatest figures he has ever seen, and his admiration is evident from this. When we talk about Britain, we must think of the famous Vickers-Armstrong Ordnance Factory. It is said that the Vickers-Armstrong factory can always see the sunlight, because Italy, Japan, Spain, Canada, Ireland, the Netherlands, and New Zealand all have Vickers-Armstrong branch factories, and its business is also the most profitable. In 1932, the major shareholders of the Vickers factory were British Chancellor of the Exchequer Sir Chamberlain, Sir Austen Chamberlain, who won the 1925 Nobel Peace Prize, and Foreign Secretary Sir Simon, but Foreign Secretary Simon sold his shares last year. When the European War broke out in 1914, many people were forced to invest, such as the great philosopher Sir Balfour, the president of the YMCA, Sir Kinnett, and the chief pastor of St. Paul's Church, Angie, and three other priests were forced to invest in the Vickers factory. Sir Snowden (the Labor government's finance minister at the time had not yet been knighted) said in Congress, "If you throw a stone at the seat on the opposite side, it is impossible not to hurt a shareholder of an arms factory." Not long ago, when the war between Bolivia and Paraguay was still fierce, according to the spokesman of the authorities, "British ordnance factories freely supply ordnance to the two belligerent countries." The Times and the Manchester Guardian came out and made sharp remarks, scolding it as a fallacy, but this protest quickly subsided without a sound. In fact, the British government is unable to restrain these ordnance factories, and the latter do whatever they want, while the former humbly tolerates. The Vickers factory is like this, and the ordnance factories of various countries are also like this. Consider the French Schneider-Creusot Ordnance Company, whose owner is Mr. Schneider, who is the mastermind of hundreds of military supply warehouses in Europe. Then consider the Czech Skoda Company and the American ordnance warehouses. Before the European War, the Krupp Ordnance Factory supplied ordnance to 52 countries. During the war, it resisted the world on its own. After the war, it was bound by the Treaty of Versailles. The Krupp factory only makes locomotives, bridges, railway and other materials. In addition to the major ordnance factories we have already mentioned, there are still a large number of large and small arsenals. When the world's economic panic is at its height, the trade and export of its ordnance and ordnance suddenly increase sharply. Since 1928, the trade in ordnance has almost doubled. Mr. Kobayashi Ichizo, the director of the first-class Japanese company Tokyo Electric Power Company, said frankly, "The military industry of various countries is very prosperous. The war,

Raw materials can supply the needs of any scope for a while, and commodities cannot fill the market, so their prices are fortunate to be exempt from fluctuations and declines. This is a special nature of war raw materials, and it is also what we pay attention to." The above-mentioned major ordnance factories firmly grasp the whole of Europe in their palms, and grasp it very tightly, and bind it very severely. Those who talk about disarmament are purely empty theories that can only win the hearts of ordinary people. Unless the governments stop this kind of activity that destroys and ruins mankind, otherwise, if they increase their activity, there may be a war in the near future. These ordnance manufacturers are truly the enemies of peace, the enemies of progress, and the enemies of culture. Therefore, ordnance manufacturing should be restrained, so that the world can regain the dawn of peace from the terrible war.

General Situation of Rural Finance in the Country

(Nanjing) The Central Agricultural Experimental Institute investigated the rural financial situation in 871 counties in 22 provinces. (A) Merchants are the largest source of loans and savings, accounting for 25%. Mortgage credit is more common as a credit method, accounting for 46.3%. The interest rate on loans is as high as 5% or more, with 2-3% being the most common, accounting for 36.2%. The loan period is mostly from June to one year, accounting for 64.7%. Banks are the fewest savings institutions, and private individuals are the most, accounting for 61.2%. (B) Mutual aid societies and cooperatives. Rolling associations are more common as types of mutual aid societies, accounting for 36%. The amount of money in the mutual aid societies is mostly below 100 yuan, accounting for 58%. The term of the mutual aid societies is mostly below five years, accounting for 57.3%. Credit cooperatives are more developed as types of cooperatives, accounting for 46.2% (Central News Agency Telegram, 13th)

(Special Telegram, 13th)

Liu Xiang Arrived in Hankou Yesterday Afternoon

Will Fly to Yichang Today, Then Transfer to Chongqing

To Go to the Front Lines to Supervise Suppression

(Hankou) Liu Xiang, traveling westward from Nanjing on the Wuxue steamer on the 10th, passed Jiujiang on the 12th, and arrived in Hankou at 11 AM on the 13th. Chief Zhang Lingjiu, representing Yu Weiyi, Qiu Jia, and others accompanied him. Liu stayed at the Central Bank and is scheduled to take a plane with Zhang Lingjiu and Zhang Biguo to Yichang on the 14th, then transfer to Chongqing to go to the front lines to supervise the suppression. Liu made a statement to reporters, roughly saying that this trip east to meet Chiang and the central authorities had resulted in concrete decisions regarding military and political affairs in Sichuan Province. In military affairs, there is a deadline to eliminate the remaining bandits. Currently, bandits in northern Sichuan are trying to flee to Sui and Xuan, resulting in fierce battles. Bandits in southern Sichuan are retreating to the border of Hunan, and the central government also has plans for suppression. After returning to Chongqing, I will go to Chengdu, and then to the front lines to make arrangements, and coordinate with the Shaanxi army for a general offensive. During this period, the central government will provide monthly aid of 800,000 yuan for bandit suppression expenses. In politics, a provincial government will be established, and finances will be reorganized. The central government will establish special commissioners to be responsible for national taxes. Finally, he said that everything he saw in Nanjing, Shanghai, and Hankou was being constructed under the guidance of Chairman Chiang and was on a grand scale, which left a very good impression. (13th Dispatch)

(Hankou) At 2 PM on the 13th, Liu Xiang went to Hanyang to visit the arsenal, accompanied by Ma Zhaoqi from the headquarters. He returned to Hankou at 4 PM. Liu is scheduled to lead Zhang Biguo and Leng Kaitai on a flight to Yichang at 10 AM on the 14th. The remaining entourage, led by Chen Songyun and others, will take three Hankou-Yichang cars to Yichang in the afternoon of the 13th and are scheduled to arrive in Yichang on the 14th, where they will join Liu on the Bayu warship to return to Sichuan. (13th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Northwestern Inspection Notes

By Our Special Correspondent, Geng Ya

Old and New Relay Stations at Yandun Completely Destroyed by War

On the 16th, going west from Gedaying, two or three consecutive stations were short on water and grass. Camels travel slowly, especially at these impoverished stations. (It is commonly said that the route from Lanzhou to Suzhou is the wealthy eighteen stations, from Suzhou to Hami is the poor ten stations, and from Hami to Dihua is the neither rich nor poor eighteen stations. The route we are taking is precisely the poorest of the poor ten stations.) Empty-bellied and carrying heavy loads, it is truly difficult to proceed. Therefore, we decided to abandon camels for horses and travel with the entangled soldiers. The journey was across an endless sandy plain, with all the riders competing to be first. Only the sound of hooves and the sight of flying sand and dust were heard and seen. In a single day, we covered an estimated 180 li. The names of the stations we passed, starting from Gedaying, are: 40 li to "Kushui Jing" (Bitter Water Well), where the water contains saltpeter and alkali, causing drinkers to immediately suffer from diarrhea, let alone the bitter taste being hard to swallow. There are more than ten broken-walled yards, where the lonely and miserable mail carriers are pitiable. 70 li to "Yaodianzi" (Waist Shop), a circle of ruined walls, with a pond of green water nearby. The thirsty horses were about to drink, but everyone stopped them with whips. One horse's nose spurted fresh blood, and its chest and feet were like stocks, bleeding profusely as it walked. 70 li to "Gezi Yandun" (Grid Beacon Tower), abbreviated as Yandun. We dismounted to rest. The carcasses of dead horses and camels were constantly seen along the way, especially in the Yaodianzi section, where an average of one camel or horse died every four telegraph poles. It is said that on the thousand-li journey to Anxi and Hami, an average of one camel or horse dies every three li, totaling as many as 340 or 350 animals. The poverty of the "poor stations" can be imagined. However, if each station had shops with complete grass and fodder, and the camel drivers and owners did not abuse the animals, the deaths of camels and horses would not be so severe. That night, we arrived at Yandun, with the clock pointing to ten o'clock. The entangled soldiers led us to the home of a postal worker, where we piled our bedding on his heated kang (brick bed). In front of the kang was a stove, burning firewood vigorously, with the bottom end connected to the heated kang. Tea was being cooked on the stove.

Long Liushui Ka Long "Tuokute Man", aged 48, who could speak Chinese, was always by our side. According to him, his job is to specifically check travelers passing through. If they do not have a passport, they must be turned back. Since Ma Zhongying's two disturbances in Xinjiang in the 20th year, many poor people from Xinjiang have brought their families to the interior, fleeing to Long Liushui. If those without passports are turned back, then Hami City is still three stations away. They will have no way to survive after trekking through the Gobi Desert, which violates the law. Applying for a passport in Hami costs about several dozen taels of silver per person, which is not a big deal, but it requires submitting an application to the provincial government for approval by telegram, which is quite troublesome. Later, company commander "Tun Lan Kele" and others went out to feed the horses, and the Ka Long (checkpoint chief) held the reporter's hand again and said, "Sir, (a common form of address in Xinjiang) I want to make friends with you. When you meet Director Yao (Dr. Le), please tell him that 'Tuokute Man Man Ka Long is a good person, and Tuokute Man Man Ka Long also says Director Yao is a good person, and Young Director (Yao's son) is also a good person.' I am called

Tuokute Man Man Ka Long, please remember it firmly." Seeing his sincere attitude, although the reporter wanted to explain something, at least he had to explain that he dared not falsely assume the title of "Sir," but he did not want to disappoint or spoil his mood. Moreover, he had repeatedly told him about the reporter's mission, but he still seemed not to understand, so he had to nod in response to this ridiculous request, doing him a favor. He immediately looked triumphant, stroked his beard, and leaned back, but unexpectedly, a slight resistance like human movement suddenly occurred under the bedding he was leaning on. He seemed to sense something was amiss and asked with a cough, "Is it a cat?" The postman, hearing this, gave an irrelevant answer, calling out, "Get up, get up, let the adults sleep on the kang for a night!" Then, a young woman's head, with an displeased expression, lazily emerged from the bedding, seemingly still trying to put on clothes in the bedding. The Ka Long immediately spat on the ground and said, "Oh, sorry, I'm just an old man." He then jumped down from the kang, and the reporter also went outside to walk in the moonlight. There were about six or seven houses in the neighboring area, and the beams and rafters had all been dismantled and burned, leaving not a single complete room to live in. The bright moon shone askew, making us feel even more desolate. The well water in Yandun has a slight bitter taste, and there is a small amount of grassland nearby that can be used for wheat fields, but strong winds often blow, easily damaging crops. All grains and fodder from the stations west of Xingxingxia come from Qin City. Qin City is located on the southern slope of the Tianshan Mountains, where snowmelt can be used for irrigation, the land is fertile, and the agricultural production is abundant. The city is inhabited by farmers and merchants, with an estimated two hundred and several dozen Han households, totaling over a thousand people. There was a proposal to establish an Yiwu County in the 20th year, but unfortunately, the incident broke out, and the entire city was massacred, with less than one or two out of ten people surviving. As a result, fields and gardens were abandoned, and houses were in ruins. The stations that relied on the city for food supplies now have to seek supplies from Anxi and Hami even further away. However, the sandy land in each station is not entirely incapable of growing vegetables and wheat. It is only necessary to dig deep trenches to plant what are called "cellar seedlings," which (1) can access groundwater and retain moisture, (2) can reduce and avoid wind and sand disasters, and (3) the climate must be warmer than the ground, and sunlight can still directly penetrate. Cellar seedlings have these four benefits and can thrive. Two li east of Yandun is a ruin with the remains of a beacon tower and broken walls. The surrounding sandy land has crisscrossing earth embankments, and the sand is scaly, as if it had been plowed. It is said that this was the old Yandun relay station, which was moved to its present location after the Tongzhi Rebellion. Unexpectedly, it was destroyed by Ma Zhongying again. To restore the old appearance, in view of the current situation, it cannot be done in three or five years. Before Li, he put forward a condition, saying that as long as Tang Shixia completely returns the valuable items privately pledged by Tang to a certain bank to the Wang family, everything can be discussed. Tang Shixia had some difficulties with this, so the matter was shelved. The reason for Zai's concern is that the antiques secretly pledged by Tang to a certain bank will mature next summer, with the outstanding interest already reaching a huge 110,000 yuan. Among them are four pairs of the most precious agate bowls, which were tributes from Siam during the Jiaqing era. Antique dealers who have seen them said that each bowl can be worth three or four thousand yuan, and even more if sold to Westerners. In addition, there are many exquisite gold-inlaid jade items. The bank is planning to ship them to London after maturity to sell them at a good price. If this batch of antiques flows into Europe and America, it will be the second major loss of national treasures worthy of the attention of the Chinese people after the theft of antiques from the Forbidden City to Paris. It is reported that the authorities in Beiping and Tianjin have conducted some investigations and are preparing to closely monitor and detain these antiques when they are exported. (11th)

Fujian-Jiangxi-Guangdong Border Designated as Pacification Zone

Guangdong's Military Suppression of Bandits Comes to an End

Shantou Communication: After the remnants of the Red bandits fled west, the local order in the Fujian-Jiangxi border area gradually recovered. Western Fujian, including Shanghang, Wuping, and Yongding, was originally garrisoned by Huang Renhuan's division of the Guangdong Army, which has recently returned to defend the Guangdong border. The Second Brigade, consisting of Li Hengzhong and Wu Hanping's two regiments, returned to Jiaoling on the 4th. The southern Jiangxi area has been designated as the Sixth Pacification Zone, with Yu Hanmou as the Pacification Commissioner, overseeing the ten counties of Ganzhou, Nankang, Zhiyou, Chongyi, Xinfeng, Anyuan, Longnan, Dingnan, Qiannan, and Xunwu. Junmenling, originally belonging to Huichang County, belongs to the Fifth Zone. Luotang and below belong to Xunwu. Chen Cheng's troops have moved south from Ruijin to take over the defense. All previous organizations for supply stations and combat operations have come to an end. The troops stationed in the Chaozhou and Meizhou counties have also been working hard on pacification, actively organizing local guard teams, and focusing on security construction. (7th)

Anqing Repairs City Walls and Builds Bunkers

Organizing a City Defense Works Committee

Levying Commercial Donations and Rent

Anqing Communication: When Jin Youshu was the head of the Anqing Municipal Preparatory Office years ago, he dismantled the city walls around the northeast gates and opened roads to promote the prosperity of the city of Anqing. In recent years, bandit alarms have been frequent, and the authorities have temporarily added defense works to the dismantled areas. Recently, Sun Peifang, the magistrate of Huaining County, following Chairman Chiang's orders, invited gentry and businessmen from the provincial capital to form the Anqing City Defense Works Committee to repair the remaining city walls. This has been approved by the provincial government, and it is proposed to levy commercial donations in the city, collecting a quarter of the annual business tax at once. In addition, one month's rent will be collected from the city, borne by the landlords, and paid in two installments by the tenants, each time deducting half a month from the rent they should pay. The receipt for the payment will be used to offset the rent due to the landlords. The City Defense Committee will assign donation collectors, carrying receipts, and members of the Public Security Bureau will be dispatched to collect the donations. The committee is now actively surveying, soliciting bids from merchants, and preparing for construction. The county government has issued a notice urging merchants and people to pay the commercial donations and rent donations. The rent donations will be paid in November and December. If the November rent has already been paid to the landlords, it should be postponed from November to January 1935, and the tenants should still deduct it from the rent they should pay, so as to collect one month's rent, so that the two projects of repairing the city walls and building bunkers can be completed as soon as possible. (11th)

Guangdong News Industry Holds Memorial Service for Shi Liangcai

All Organizations Sent Representatives to Attend

To Encourage Continued Spirit of Mr. Shi

Guangzhou Communication: On the 9th of this month, the Guangdong Newspaper Industry Association, the Guangdong Provincial Journalists' Association, and the Guangzhou Journalists' Association held a memorial service for Mr. Shi Liangcai, General Manager of the Shanghai Shen Bao, in the auditorium of the Provincial Public Education Center on Zhonghua North Road. On that day, six or seven hundred people from the entire news industry and journalists attended, and organizations such as the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, the Provincial Party Headquarters, the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Guangdong Machinery Industry Association, and Fangbian Hospital sent representatives to attend. The orphanage's silver band played music at the scene, and the atmosphere was solemn and tragic. The meeting began at noon. Students from the orphanage played mournful music. The presidium and representatives of the organizations took their seats separately. The entire assembly saluted the party and national flag, then bowed three times to Mr. Shi Liangcai's portrait and observed three minutes of silence. After reading the memorial oration, the chairman delivered the opening address and reported on Mr. Shi's life. Next, Tan Huiquan, the representative of the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, delivered a speech, roughly saying that today is Mr. Shi's memorial service, and he was ordered to attend, feeling infinite grief. Moreover, the assassination of Mr. Shi gave rise to infinite thoughts. Mr. Shi worked hard in the news industry for more than ten years and achieved remarkable results, both using newspapers as the mouthpiece of the people and promoting cultural and social undertakings to seek happiness for the people. His great courage deserves to be a mentor to the people. The success of Mr. Shi's career benefited society, but unexpectedly, he was shot and killed by violent thugs on his way back from Haining. The reasons for the assassination and the identity of the murderers have not yet been solved. The thugs' disregard for the military police, their disregard for the law, and their indiscriminate killing of people are truly enemies of humanity. Mr. Shi devoted his life to promoting the evolution of society and seeking happiness for the people. His death seems to be without regret, but Mr. Shi's death is still a great loss to today's society. However, it is hoped that the news industry will continue Mr. Shi's past spirit and work together, so that today's memorial service for Mr. Shi will have meaning and value. After the speech, guests such as Zhou Qiying delivered speeches. Finally, mournful music was played again, and the meeting dispersed in solemnity. The memorial oration and elegiac couplets from various circles are omitted.

Puyi's Sister-in-Law, Tang Shixia's Treachery

The Story of Tang's Separation and Reunion with Her Husband Pujie

Will Act as a Female Spy to Pledge Allegiance to the Puppet Organization

Beiping Communication: Tang Shixia, the wife of Pujie, the younger brother of Puyi, the puppet ruler of Northeast China, is known in Beiping society as the Second Grandma Pujie. When the puppet organization was first established the year before last, she once gave a speech, frankly discussing with reporters in Beiping and Tianjin that "the puppet regime is completely a puppet of the Japanese, and I personally absolutely stand as a Chinese, and from a patriotic perspective, I will strive to oppose Puyi in the future, and divorce Pujie to show my determination." Her outspokenness was well-known at the time. Even today, when people talk about her, they still regard her as a fashionable noblewoman. Yesterday, I met an official who was closely related to the former Regent's Palace and learned about Tang Shixia's words and actions over the years and her recent secret activities, which are also related to the political situation in the puppet regime. Here is a description as follows: After Tang Shixia stole and sold a large number of important cultural relics and antiques from the former Regent's Palace in Beiping last year, she secretly pledged the remaining treasures (including the Song edition of the Thirteen Classics, which is related to culture, and Wang Xizhi's calligraphy) to a foreign bank in Dongjiaomin Lane, obtaining 400,000 yuan. She then took her male companion, a certain Mr. Si, and several personal servants, left Beiping for Shanghai. On the way, she hired two foreign warriors as bodyguards, and whenever passing through land and water checkpoints, these

large numbers of boxes and cages were rarely inspected because the two foreigners came forward to claim that they belonged to foreigners. After arriving in Shanghai, they secretly rented a large house on a certain road, and their whereabouts seemed to be less active, but the meaning was very secretive. Zaiyi, the former Regent who was trapped in the Beiping Wang Mansion, was afraid that Tang would ruin the family reputation and flee with the money, and that she would come to Beiping again to thoroughly extort money, so he reported it to the Public Security Bureau. On the one hand, he opened a list of the stolen antiques and treasures, requesting an investigation, and on the other hand, he reported all the existing public property and valuable items in the mansion, requesting that they be registered and protected. At the same time, he secretly transferred the grand mansion and private deposits in the Shichahai area to a certain foreigner and voluntarily paid a large amount of protection money each month, begging the foreigner to forcibly and illegally occupy the property in his name to prevent Tang's covetousness. According to Zaiyi's investigation, after Tang Shixia lived in Shanghai, she had a relationship with a young man surnamed Wang and changed her name to Shi Fenjia. This summer, she openly went to Qingdao with Wang to escape the heat. Before long, her relationship with Wang soured, and she went to Dalian alone. Later, unable to bear the monotonous life, she longed for a reconciliation with her husband Pujie, so she wrote to her father-in-law Zaiyi (Puyi's relative), elaborately explaining that her previous statement of loyalty to the Republic of China and scolding the puppet regime was a self-preservation and a means of protecting the property of the Beiping Mansion. In fact, her heart was still extremely loyal, and since she was ultimately Pujie's wife, she wanted to use a mask to operate between the Republic of China and the puppet regime, trying to contribute to Puyi, and so on. Zaiyi, upon receiving the letter, understood that Tang Shixia intended to undo what had been done, but Zaiyi deeply disapproved, so he wrote to his son Pujie, strongly urging him not to be

fooled by her. Pujie, hearing that his wife had expressed a desire to repent, could not

suppress his old affection, so he secretly went to Dalian from Changchun. After meeting, they cohabited, but ultimately, due to the fierce opposition from his parents-in-law and the puppet emperor Puyi's entourage, the reunion could not be realized. Seeing that this plan was difficult to sell, Tang Shixia changed her approach and eagerly wanted to do espionage work to gain merit and be seen by the puppet regime, and then negotiate with the Pujie family, hoping that the couple's reconciliation could be promoted by political power. With Tang's plan decided, she recently returned to Tianjin again, accompanied by several transformed guards from both the Japanese and puppet regimes, who provided protection along the way. After arriving in Tianjin, she stayed in the Asahi Street in the Japanese concession and acted unusually secretly. According to those who have seen Tang Shixia, Tang claims that her recent activities have been well received by the puppet regime, but she desperately hopes to cooperate with her husband Pujie and hopes for the understanding of her father-in-law. After this news spread, the remnants of the Qing Dynasty (because most of the surviving elders residing in Beiping and Tianjin are in the Northeast) came forward to mediate for Zai

Songjiang: Xi Chan Temple Monk Forcibly Seizes Fenglong Temple Property

The Xi Chan Temple monk Lan Feng, in regards to the issue of forcibly seizing the property of the Fenglong Temple, falsely accused the principal of Bailong Elementary School to the county court, alleging that the principal had instructed school workers to obstruct his freedom. Although the prosecutor's office had determined that there was no supporting evidence and declined to prosecute, monk Lan Feng, not giving up, appealed to the High Court for reconsideration, which ordered a retrial. Investigations reveal that the Fenglong Temple has historically been local government property, as recorded in the county chronicles. Later, because the temple was not regularly worshiped and lacked incense offerings, monks from Xi Chan Temple took it upon themselves to renovate it and convert it into monk quarters, claiming to be in charge and effectively seizing it. Last year, due to the increasing number of students at Bailongtan Elementary School and the inadequacy of school buildings, the school petitioned the education bureau, which forwarded the request to the provincial government. After deliberation, it was approved to allocate the temple to the school for use, with appropriate compensation to Lan Feng for renovation expenses. The school proceeded with the takeover and submitted a report to the education bureau for review and record. Simultaneously, it obtained approval from the education bureau to hire workers for construction. Unexpectedly, the monk continued to insist on the issue of ownership, falsely claiming that the original sixth-grade classroom of the school belonged to Xi Chan Temple, and falsely accused the school of encroachment in the county court. After several interrogations, the case was dismissed due to insufficient evidence. Undeterred, the monk repeatedly gathered monks, arbitrarily destroyed the fence built on the land, and engaged in vandalism and harassment, assaulting people. At the same time, he used a large brick to injure a school worker. The school worker, in self-defense, slightly resisted. The monk then colluded with incense-offering patrons to accuse the school principal of instructing the school worker to obstruct his freedom. After investigation, it was found that the principal had no criminal suspicion and was again not prosecuted. Unable to implicate the principal, the monk again appealed to the High Court for reconsideration. Now, all the teachers and students of the school believe that monk Lan Feng is intentionally creating trouble and undermining education, and have sent public letters to their fellow villagers in Beijing and Shanghai, calling for united support for justice.

Ye Zongcheng Dies of Illness in His Hometown

Ye Zongcheng, the director of the First National Tax Collection Office of this county, was previously reported for corruption in the conversion of rice into tribute grain. After being reported by local people, he was summoned and detained, and Yang Yunwen was appointed as the new director. Later, the provincial committee conducted an investigation and ordered Director Ye to progressively remit the funds, with the assurance of guarantee from Lu Longxiang, director of the fund production office, and Li Zongtai, the sixth district chief, and were approved by the department order. He was ordered to go to his hometown to collect the tributes of rice and grain in order to end this case. Unexpectedly, Ye requested to send two political police officers to Yang Luming's home in Caojing, but he did not know why he died at Yang's house this morning. It is said to be caused by phlegm asthma. The telegram county government transferred to the county court, prosecutor Zhu to go to the township for inspection. Ye's family members have also hired a car to go to the township to take care of the funeral.

Jiang Zhuang Villagers Robbed

Chen Ruitang's home, a villager in the eleventh village of Jiang Zhuang, in the eighth district, was robbed by more than a dozen bandits with local accents at about 12 o'clock the night before. They carried box guns, iron rulers, and other items, and forcibly robbed him of more than fifty single and lined garments, three silver bracelets, forty bolts of cloth, five leather jackets, and nine hemp sacks. Before leaving, they also beat the homeowner's son, A Jin, in the face and fled southeast. The area public office has reported to the county and asked for an arrest.

Suzhou: Another Robbery Occurs in Suzhou City

Ma Chengji's soil plaster shop, number 52, in Bifengfang Lane, Zhongbi Palace Lane, Suzhou City, was suddenly entered by six burly men at about 7 pm on the 12th. All of them spoke with local accents. Four of them held handguns and rushed in, silencing anyone who tried to make a sound. They searched at will and robbed more than ninety taels of opium, more than one hundred and eighty silver dollars, more than one hundred and sixteen small silver coins, and various fractional notes and copper coins, and then fled with the loot. After the incident, the public security bureau ordered each branch office and station to conduct a night-long investigation and to check suspicious persons at each city gate, but to no avail. After investigation by various stations, more than ten suspects with suspicious appearances, including Wang Wanqing, Qian Damaizi, Yin Desheng, Shan Zhanyun, Xiao Lao Jiu, Xiao Haizhou, and Yao Zaisheng, were arrested and are being interrogated separately. The county government has reported to the Department of Civil Affairs for review and handling yesterday (the 13th). Since entering winter, four robberies have occurred in Suzhou City in less than two months. Residents with some wealth are all uneasy.

Peng Gongfu Returns to Suzhou

Peng Gongfu, a famous painter from Wumen, was previously recommended by the Zheng She Painting and Calligraphy Association to go to Peiping to organize the Zheng She Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition, which was highly praised by all sectors. Recently, the Wuxian sojourner's association in Beijing held an opening ceremony and invited Zheng She to exhibit. Peng was also entrusted to collect exhibits in Beijing, obtaining more than a hundred pieces of exquisite works, which he brought back to participate. Now that the event is over, he said he will return to Suzhou. It is said that after a little rest, he must respond to the invitations from members in Hankou, Guangdong, Japan, and other places, and go to hold exhibitions in turn.

Wuxi: Strict Prohibition of Extortion of Disaster Relief Fees

The county government of this county has, in response to repeated provincial orders regarding the autumn disaster this year, stipulated that the county-wide general reduction should be the primary measure, preventing malpractices. Only completely barren fields should be exempted in full. Orders were issued to various districts to compile registers of barren land. Although the registers from various districts have been submitted, some districts have not yet finalized them, so they have not been announced. The original report from the district chiefs was for more than 225,000 mu, but after officials from the finance, civil affairs, and construction departments of the province came to Wuxi and conducted a joint survey with the county, the area was determined to be more than 148,000 mu. The procedures for verification and elimination are very complicated. Unexpectedly, district secretaries and map officials are using this as a means of making money, extorting barren land fees, reporting cultivated land as barren, and reporting barren land as cultivated, leading to numerous malpractices. The villagers are complaining and repeatedly submitting complaints to the county government. Yesterday, in addition to issuing a public notice strictly prohibiting such practices, the county government also instructed the district chiefs to promptly investigate and find out those who have been extorted, ordering the original handlers to refund all the money; otherwise, they should report them truthfully for legal action.

Disputes over Extortion by Xicheng Company

The Xicheng long-distance bus company has been repeatedly complained about by passengers because of the unfairness of the prescribed fares. Once, Bian Shang and other merchants and residents of Qingyang, at the junction of Xicheng, submitted a report to the provincial government. Unexpectedly, one wave has not subsided, and another wave has risen. Yesterday, Chen Shengfu and Feng, two men from Yueqiao, Cheng, were holding round-trip tickets from the company. When they were about to take a bus back to Cheng at the Xizhan station, they were dragged down by the ticket inspector, saying that the ticket was out of date. Later, they were forced to go to the ticket office and pay four small silver coins per person. After Chen and others arrived, they said that the ticket had not expired, and that the company was extorting money. Therefore, they went to the town to report the information to the Second District Party Department, and then made serious negotiations with the Xicheng Company. I don’t know how to solve it.

Injury of Police Officer in Gambling Arrest Case to be Handled by the Court

Jin Bingchun, a patrol officer from the Anzhen Zhi Ba branch station, led police officers to arrest gamblers in the Zhou San Wang and Lin teahouses in Donghutang. Suddenly, a commotion broke out, and there was a conflict with the local defense corps. Both sides opened fire, and stray bullets accidentally injured police officer Su Kan (i.e., Su Sanbao) and beat Chen Lixiang and two others, which aroused a strike by the town's stores. Yesterday, Patrol Officer Jin came to the city from the countryside and reported the information to the public security bureau. Director Chen sent an official letter to the local branch court's prosecutor's office, requesting an injury examination. The chief prosecutor Qian sent a prosecutor and a coroner to the township to examine the injuries and ordered them to return home and seek medical treatment. At the same time, the county government also dispatched Zhu Wenying, the captain of the second squadron of the security team, and twenty soldiers to the scene of the incident to investigate. It was found that there were more than a dozen bullet holes in the wall of Wang Helin's house and several blood stains on the ground. The injured police officer Su Kan is being treated at Chen Tonghui's clinic. The prosecutor also confirmed the injury. After the town leader Wu Shouhuan and Captain Zhu persuaded them, half of the town's stores had resumed business as usual. The remaining stores are still on strike because the case has not been resolved. According to the merchants and residents of the area, the 22nd squadron of the defense corps does not have handguns, only rifles. The bullet holes that injured the police officer were caused by a handgun, which is probably a police accident injury. The case is now being handled by the court.

Jiangyin: Bandit Wanted in Taixing Captured in Cheng

Lu Shuxue, also known as Ma Dacheng, from Bachigou, Fifth District, Taixing, is 31 years old. He joined the bandit gang in the 18th and 19th years of the Republic of China. Under Li Fang (who has been executed), he participated in riots, burning, looting, and doing everything. Later, because of the tight arrest, Lu hid in the port area and became friends with the blind Tao, who opened a rattan shop, and became intimate with Liu Zhang, marrying her as his wife. Lu still went out as a bandit from time to time, returning with plenty of loot and savings. Those who did not know thought he was a businessman. This year, in the eighth month of the lunar calendar, because his whereabouts were known in the port area, he came to Jiang and lived in the Fengyuantai Rattan Shop at Xiaoxiangkou, Beiwai, renting a house from Zhang Rugen, who owned a barber shop. He disguised himself as a peanut factory cloth merchant to avoid attention. Later, after being detected by the Taixing County Government, on the 8th of this month, police officers were sent to Jiang to assist in the arrest. His friend sent a message to escape, only the rattan shop owner Feng Tongfu was taken away. The shop thought that Feng was implicated for no reason, so they went out to find out. Yesterday (the 12th) at 4 pm, Su Lingen, an apprentice from Chenbi Lane, Nanwai, saw Lu standing on the bow of a small boat in the Meijia Shuigoutou River in Banqiao. He secretly reported to the Fifth Squadron of the Nanwai Business Corps. The instructor Chen Yongsheng immediately led the members to go there. When Lu saw the situation, he tried to escape by swimming. The business corps fired a warning shot and chased him for about a mile. With the help of the villagers, Lu was captured. There were also accomplices Zhou Xiaozhang, Zhang Shuren, and Lu's mistress Liu Zhang on the boat, and they were all taken to the team headquarters. Lu confessed to being a bandit under the alias Wang Hui and having committed many crimes. He was taken to the hall that night, and after a brief interrogation by the investigation team, a long-distance call was made to the Taixing County Government, who sent police to Cheng to take him back for investigation and handling.

Provincial Inspector Investigates Gambling Case

Li Kaizhou, a police inspector from the Department of Civil Affairs of the Provincial Government, was ordered to investigate the public security facilities in Jiangyin and Jingjiang and has completed his duties. Recently, it was learned that Zhang Zhendong, a patrol officer from the Jiangyin Public Security Bureau, went to Yunting to arrest gamblers, and a conflict occurred between the police and the people. On the 11th, he went to investigate the truth and learned all the inside secrets. He returned to the city that day and reported to the province on the 12th.

Danyang: Robbery of Rice Boat Injures People

Zhu Lazi, a boatman from outside the south gate of the county, led his four sons from Jintan to Danyang with rice. When they arrived at Jinjiadu in Jiuli Town, it was getting dark, so they stopped overnight. Unexpectedly, at about 2:00 in the middle of the night, a number of robbers, each holding a sharp weapon and speaking in mixed accents, rushed onto the boat, claiming to be checking the boat. Zhu thought it was true and opened the hatch, and was slashed on the head by the robbers. He resisted the pain, causing him and one of the robbers to fall into the water. His four sons heard the sound and rushed to get up, and fought the enemy separately. However, the robbers had weapons and the number of people was far from equal, and eventually the robbers robbed the boat and escaped. Later, the robber in the water was not good at swimming and was caught on the spot. At the same time, the nearby police station heard the news and arrived with armed reinforcements, searching everywhere, and caught another robber, who was immediately taken to the county for interrogation. The two robbers, Chen Yuanlong and Chen Hetang, confessed to the robbery of the rice boat. Zhu Lazi, the boatman, was seriously injured and his life may be in danger.

Local Bully Gathers Crowd to Rob Rice, Causing Trouble

Zhang Xiao (nicknamed Mazi), Zhang Da Mao (nicknamed Xiazi), Zhang Suochuan, and others, local bullies in Maixi Village, Second District, are often colluding with unemployed vagrants to rob grain from people's fields. If they are offended, they set fire at night and burn things. The local people fear them like tigers. The night before, the local bullies gathered again and openly robbed more than ten stones of Yuandao rice. The owner shouted for help, but the neighbors were afraid of trouble and no one responded. After the local bullies divided the stolen rice, they divided it up and dried it in Zhang Rulin and others' yards, intending to dry it and sell it. The owner secretly identified the stolen goods and reported to the village chief and impartial people, inviting them to the yard to verify the stolen goods and order the workers to carry them back. Unexpectedly, the local bullies held knives and sticks and forcibly blocked them, provoking public anger. Everyone stepped forward and twisted the local bullies into the public hall, and reported to the Yanling branch station, which sent police to take the local bullies to the county.

Zhenjiang: Jiangsu Province Civilian Loan Office

Will Begin Lending Soon

Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and Zhao Dihua, Director of the Department of Finance, are concerned about the civilians of this province. In order to assist small business owners, they have proposed setting up a small loan office, which will be jointly operated by Jin Cheng, Farmers, and Jiangsu banks. Yesterday, a meeting was held at the Shanghai Jin Cheng Bank, and Wu Yunzhai, manager of Shanghai Jin Cheng Bank, Hou Houpei, deputy manager of Farmers Bank, and Tian Shitai, assistant of Jiangsu Bank, were appointed as directors of the board. Yang Zhaoxiong and Chen Qixiang were appointed as supervisors by the Department of Finance. The loan regulations and operating rules were approved, and Hou Houpei was elected as the managing director. The loan rules stipulate the use of funds, which are divided into four categories: (1) Purchasing goods or raw materials, (2) Adding tools for crafts and agricultural work, (3) Subsidies for promoting domestic goods, (4) Other production uses. Any small business owner in agriculture, industry, or commerce with a fixed address and legitimate business can apply for a loan. The general office is located at the Zhenjiang Farmers Bank, and the first office is located at the Zhenjiang Jiangsu Bank outside the city. It will be established and start lending in the near future. The minimum loan is one yuan, and the maximum shall not exceed two hundred yuan. In the future, small civilians will definitely benefit a lot. The office has a director and deputy director, who are said to be internally determined and will be announced soon.

Haimen: Haiqi Disaster Victims Organize Collective Eating Groups

This county suffered a prolonged drought this summer, and the autumn harvest was sharply reduced. Food shortages are severe in various districts, and people's hearts are panic-stricken, especially in Xiasha. Although local people have been running around and appealing to all parties for alms and relief, they have not received a penny so far. The disaster victims who lack food and clothing are forced to form groups and go out to beg for food, and incidents of harassment are heard every day. Recently, disaster victims in the north of Nanyang Village, Sixth District, organized collective eating groups to rob food from the homes of wealthy people in various villages. Disaster victims in the northeast of Qidong also responded, and the momentum is spreading rapidly. If the authorities do not provide relief urgently, the local security will be unimaginable.

Yinyang Town: Sea Bandits Land

Yinyang Town, Qidong, is located on the east coast. The day before yesterday (the 10th) afternoon, a bandit ship suddenly arrived, and more than twenty sea bandits landed with weapons, robbing food. Before leaving, they also kidnapped three villagers. When the security team received the news and rushed to pursue them, the bandits had already left.

Nantong: Prison Official Bribes on Behalf of Drug Offender

The Nantong District Commissioner's Office learned that Zheng Ge, a prison official in Haimen County, bribed on behalf of drug offender Pu Zhuping and reported it to the High Court, which dismissed Zheng Ge from his post and transferred him to the Nantong Court for trial. On the 12th, Judge Shao of the Criminal Court interrogated Zheng Ge and took him into custody pending judgment.

Yangzhou: Director of Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau Accused of Corruption

Shi Jichang, director of the Jiangyi Gaobao Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Bureau, has contracted the tobacco and alcohol tax from the provincial bureau. Since the quota has increased, the tobacco and alcohol merchants in the city and countryside are unable to pay. He once sent a letter to the county government, ordering the chairmen of the industry associations to comply with the regulations and make arrangements for payment. Subsequently, Teng Yizhai, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, mediated, and the eight industry associations, including Guanghuo, jointly recognized the tax of 1,400 silver coins per quarter. The approximately 500 shops that do not belong to the association are directly collected by the bureau. Unexpectedly, Director Shi was unable to obtain the department's license due to unpaid provincial taxes, and even imagined that the bureau would issue receipts and collect taxes from the shops. Later, fearing that people would report him, he sent staff to collect the receipts, which caused dissatisfaction among the tobacco and alcohol merchants, who questioned the bureau. It is heard that only a part of the receipts have been collected, and the merchants of the general intellectual class are unwilling to return them, as evidence of the director's corruption. At the same time, the eight industry associations, believing that Director Shi illegally collected taxes and deceived merchants, have collected evidence and submitted complaints to the Department of Finance and the Provincial Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau, requesting investigation and punishment.

Jiashan: Bandit Gang Robs Nunnery

The Beisheng Nunnery in the North City of Fengjing has always been prosperous with incense. The eight or nine young nuns in the nunnery are good at flattery, so there are many pilgrims and the income is not bad, which has been coveted by bandits. The night before, the nuns went to the countryside to worship the Buddhas, and only one old nun was left in the nunnery to guard it. At about 3:00 in the middle of the night, a group of bandits with sharp knives climbed over the wall and entered, drawing out their blades, silencing anyone who tried to make a sound, and rushing into each bedroom to search. The nine rooms were all searched, and none was spared. After obtaining the loot, the bandits roared and fled south. The total loss of silver, jewelry, and other items is no less than 3,000 yuan. The police have been notified to investigate.

Jiaxing: Appeal Rejected in Agricultural Bank Embezzlement Case

The Jiaxing County Farmers Bank reported a huge theft, but it was later discovered that there was embezzlement. Wu Heshu, the manager of the bank, fled in fear of punishment. The Jiaxing District Court investigated and interrogated the witnesses and filed a public prosecution. After the trial, Xu Shuxiang and Tu Yiran were sentenced to six months' imprisonment each, and Feng Xingsun and Chen A'fa were sentenced to two months' imprisonment each. Feng and Chen declared their dissatisfaction and appealed. After the High Court heard the case on the 22nd of last month, it ruled that the original judgment was not inappropriate, so it was rejected and the original judgment was upheld. It is learned that Feng and Chen intend to appeal to the Supreme Court.

Hangzhou: Fugitive from Shanghai Bank Captured in Hangzhou

Shen Qun, a staff member of the Shanghai Guohua Bank, absconded with 2,000 yuan last month and fled to Hangzhou with Li Rongmao, a partner in a dye factory. He used the alias Ye Keqin and stayed in a brothel in Gongbu for many days, spending extravagantly. The investigation team of the Provincial Public Security Bureau suspected his whereabouts, captured him and sent him to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation, and then transferred him to the Hangzhou County Local Court for interrogation.

Local News: Investigation of Wealthy Donations Completed

Standards to be Set Tomorrow, Then Collection Will Begin

According to the Central News Agency, the General Association for Universal Donations for Disaster Relief is working hard to handle the various procedures for banks, money shops, shops, and companies

silk and satin shops, jewelry stores, hotels, restaurants, Chinese and Western medicine stores, transportation companies, and photo studios to collect universal donations in order to raise donations widely. Starting tomorrow, universal donations from factory employees and workers will be handled separately in order to complete the collection as soon as possible. Regarding the donations from the wealthy, the investigation has been completed. Starting tomorrow, after the standards for the universal donations from the wealthy are set, a meeting will be convened to decide on the amount, and then notices will be issued to the wealthy to solicit donations. If the wealthy are stingy and do not donate or delay in responding, they will be announced in the newspaper so that the public will be aware of the warnings and find ways to deal with the wealthy misers who do not give to charity.

Railway Department and Others Donate Eight Aircraft; Test Flight at Hongqiao Yesterday

Officers to Fly to Beijing on the 15th

To Attend Naming Ceremony on the 16th

According to the Central News Agency, the Railway Department and the employees of various state-owned railways under its jurisdiction donated about one million yuan for aviation to save the country and purchased eight "Corsair" reconnaissance planes from the Curtiss Company in the United States. They were shipped here a few days ago and assembled at the airport factory in Hongqiao, Shanghai. The plane is a biplane, the whole body is silver-gray, the tail is blue and white, and the wings are painted with the Kuomintang emblem of the blue sky and white sun. The names of the railways donating are painted on both sides of the fuselage, including "Jinghu, Hangyong", "Jiaoji Pingsui", "Zhengtai", "Longhai", "Beining", "Jinpu" and "Railway No. 1", "Railway No. 2" and other eight aircraft. After each aircraft was assembled, a test flight was conducted yesterday morning. Air school instructors Li Huaimin and Wang Changli came to Shanghai from Hangzhou the night before to drive. After the drivers arrived at the airport yesterday morning, they first]

inspected the parts of each aircraft, and then started the engines. At 10:00 a.m., each aircraft took off one after another and performed various combat flights until noon. However, "Jinghu Hangyong" and "Beining" were test-flown in the afternoon because the paint was not dry. It is heard that after the test flight, the planes will remain in the airport until the 15th, when the officers will fly to Beijing to participate in the naming ceremony to be held on the 16th. In the future, famous planes will have to perform along the donation lines to arouse the public's interest in aviation. It is heard that when the test flight was conducted yesterday morning, Xia Xiaoxia, a member of the Renqing Memorial School Preparatory Committee, and Zhang Youjun, a staff member, visited the scene.

Aviation Donation Award Ceremony

Rescheduled for the 29th

Location Also Changed to Lake Society

Wu Tiecheng, the leader of the solicitation team of the China Aviation Association, held a second meeting yesterday afternoon to prepare for the award ceremony. The International Hotel, which was decided at the last meeting as the venue, was changed to the Lake Society because the venue was insufficient. The details of the meeting are as follows:

Meeting Held Yesterday Afternoon

The second preparatory meeting for the award ceremony was held at 4:00 p.m. yesterday on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge Youth Association. Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Yao Xijiu, Zhang Yuliang, Chen Chengzhi, Mao Heyuan, Li Boyuan, Fang Zhicheng, and others attended. Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao) chaired the meeting and Zhang Yuliang took the minutes. After the formalities were completed, the chairman reported that the International Hotel, which was decided at the previous meeting as the venue, had been contacted, but the large dining room was not sufficient for the use of a large meeting of thousands of people, so it was proposed to change it. The previously set date was also proposed to be postponed due to the preparation procedures, which may not be enough. Please pay for discussion.

Discussion Results

(1) The venue will be changed to the Guizhou Road Lake Society; (2) The date will be changed to 2:00 p.m. on the 29th of this month; (3) Admission will be by invitation only, limited to 1,000 copies (celebrities from all walks of life, team leaders, agencies, schools, groups); (4) Groups, team leaders, and individuals with excellent achievements will be awarded certificates in addition to medals; (5) The Aviation Association, the Municipal Government, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Education Bureau, the General Labor Union, and the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association will each send five people to be in charge of the reception, and a platoon of 30 Boy Scouts will be sent to maintain order at the venue; (6) The general affairs will be handled by the representatives attending the preparatory meeting; (7) 300 servings of refreshments will be reserved; (8) The next preparatory meeting will be held at 3:00 p.m. on the 28th of this month at the Lake Society. The meeting adjourned at about 6:00 p.m.

Jian De Bank's Reorganization Failed: Public Notice of Closure Begins Yesterday

Entrust Accountants and Lawyers to Issue Public Notice

Schedule an Extraordinary Shareholders' Meeting

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Jian De Commercial Savings Bank, after suspending business for five days starting from the 8th of this month, failed to reach an agreement on reorganization through consultation. The board of directors decided to close the business and liquidate according to the law. Details are as follows:

Reorganization Failed. After the Jian De Bank suspended business, a meeting of old and new shareholders was held to reorganize. A final discussion was held at the board of directors meeting on the 12th of this month. However, the conditions for the new shareholder Zhu Hegao and others to join could not be agreed upon, making it impossible to continue business. A decision was made to close the business, and accountants Pan Xulun, lawyer Cai Liucheng, and lawyer Qu Yue were entrusted to issue a public notice of the closure on behalf of the bank.

Public Notice of Closure. Accountant Pan Xulun, lawyer Cai Liucheng, and lawyer Qu Yue, representing Jian De Bank Co., Ltd., announced a public notice of temporary suspension of business, stating: "According to the Jian De Bank Co., Ltd. board of directors' entrustment, the bank previously suspended business from the 8th of this month due to internal reorganization. The board of directors’ meeting on the 12th of this month resolved that there was still no way to maintain the business and had to continue the temporary suspension. In addition to reporting according to the law, we were asked to request your esteemed accountants and lawyers to issue a public notice on its behalf, as above. December 13, 1934, Republic of China."

Liquidation Pending. After the Jian De Bank announced its closure, a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency learned that the total amount of fixed-term deposits and promissory note loans was approximately 180,000 yuan, and the total amount of savings was approximately 30,000 yuan. The total amount owed to others was approximately 210,000 yuan. It was decided to wait until after the shareholders' meeting before entrusting an accountant to verify the accounts and handle liquidation matters.

Shareholders' Meeting Called. Jian De Bank scheduled an extraordinary shareholders' meeting for 2:00 PM on the 29th of this month at the Lixin Accounting Firm, No. 190 Ningbo Road, Shanghai, to discuss the way forward. All shareholders have been notified to attend on time. As for the creditors, they have also entrusted lawyers to pursue their claims according to the law.

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that sources related to Guangxi province in this city recently received a victory telegram from the Guilin headquarters of the Guangxi bandit suppression army, which stated: "(1) Although the communist bandits claim to have more than 100,000 people in this all-out westward flight, they took an offensive posture after passing through southern Jiangxi and southern Hunan, and stayed in Yizhang for more than ten days, showing a leisurely attitude. Even Yan Sengwu's battalion defeated Dong Zhentang's division of the pseudo-Fifth Army Corps and captured more than 600 people, which shows the bandits' panic. Our army has dispatched large detachments to pursue and suppress them, hoping to join forces with friendly Hunan and Guizhou forces to attack and annihilate them. Guilin Headquarters, Jia Xu."

After the Closure of the Private Postal Bureaus: Post Office Expands Facilities

Central News Agency reports that the national private postal bureaus' petition to cease operations was described in detail in yesterday's newspaper. A reporter made a special trip to the Postal Administration to investigate. According to the spokesman of the General Post Office, there were 386 private postal bureaus nationwide that registered with the post office and obtained licenses. However, 23 of them have voluntarily ceased operations this year, so there are actually only 363 remaining. Among them, Jiangxi has 14, Guangdong has 26, Fujian has 23, Shandong has 6, Hebei has 14, Sichuan has 4, Zhejiang has 40, Hubei has 16, Jiangsu and Anhui have 161, and Shanghai has 49. If each bureau employs an average of three or four people, there are approximately 1,000 employees in total. Although there are branches in various places, most are managed by one family and also operate other businesses. In February of this year, the General Post Office was ordered to instruct the private postal bureaus in various places to gradually cease operations by the end of this year. After that, a general order was issued to all district postal offices

Municipal Party Headquarters Submits to the Central Government: Please Ban Empty Banks

Bankruptcies Are Often Heard Of

Sufficient to Disrupt Finance

The Municipal Party Headquarters submitted a document to the Central Executive Committee yesterday, stating: "Submitting a case for forwarding. According to the report submitted by the Third District Party Headquarters affiliated to this association, it is believed that banks are the highest financial institutions, used to regulate the economy and stabilize society. How their capital should be sufficient is known to all. In recent times, the economy has collapsed, and all industries have declined. As a result, banks are the first to bear the brunt. Those with strong capital have no problems, but those who are usually empty are inevitably in danger. Therefore, various savings categories are widely established, or even high interest rates are offered to attract customers and make up for losses. However, transferring from east to west inevitably leads to inadequate resources. Therefore, bankruptcies are often heard of, disrupting society and harming the people, which is by no means insignificant. For this reason, the 88th Party Member Congress of the affiliated sub-department resolved to submit a request to your association to forward to the central government and the executive院,派members to conduct a thorough investigation of the capital of banks nationwide. If they are insufficient, take measures to rectify them, or order them to liquidate within a time limit, so as to ensure the stability of the social economy and prevent the people from suffering from bankruptcy, which is a public convenience, etc. Based on this, it is believed that the bankruptcy of banks that are not substantial has a very bad influence on the entire economy and harms society and the public. At a time when the national economy is declining and international finance is turbulent, if thorough investigation and suppression are not carried out, once flaws arise, what consequences will be left behind? Therefore, after the 98th Standing Committee meeting of this association, it was decided to forward it to the Municipal Executive Committee for discussion and recording. It is reasonable to submit a document to your association for review and approval, and to request your approval to forward it to the central government and forward it to the Executive院 for a thorough investigation to stabilize finance and benefit society, which is a party convenience, etc. According to this, it is found that what is said is indeed the truth. In addition to replying, it is reasonable to submit a document for forwarding, and to request your association to review and handle it, which is a party convenience. Sincerely submit to the Central Executive Committee", and so on.

Appeal to Party, Government, and Military Agencies for Assistance

Take the Evening Train to Beijing to Petition the Central National Government

The National Private Postal Bureaus closed for one day yesterday, organized a petition group, and held a large-scale petition, requesting a postponement of the closure and maintaining the livelihood of employees. That night, they went to Beijing to unite with representatives from various places to appeal to the院 and departments. The details are as follows:

National Shutdown

There are approximately 500 private postal bureaus nationwide. The Ministry of Communications ordered the private postal bureaus to close down uniformly by the end of 1934. Therefore, a petition group was organized, and they closed for one day yesterday to hold a petition. Various private postal bureaus in the north and south of Shanghai, such as Quansheng, Furun Song, Xinggong, Rishengsheng, Senchang, Yuxingfu, Yuxingkang, Renchang, Taigujin, Zhengdayuan, Zhenghexie, Zhengda, etc., were all closed. The words "Petition by the Industry, Closed for One Day" were posted at the entrance.

Petition to Party and Government

After representatives from private postal bureaus across the country arrived in Shanghai one after another, they gathered at the Xinyegongsuo in Li Xian Gua Street at 9:00 AM yesterday, hired three large trucks, and set off to hold a petition. Approximately 200 representatives wore white cloth signs that read "Private Postal Bureaus Petition." They first went to the city center to petition the Municipal Government and the Social Affairs Bureau. When the petition truck passed the Songhu Road and the Public Security Branch Bureau in the city center, the chief of the branch ordered a general representative to go to the Municipal Government. As for the petition truck and petitioners, they all stayed in front of the branch.

What Happened

Both agreed to report and handle the matter after consulting with their superiors. At 1:00 PM, they went to the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters at Fenglin Bridge to petition, where Dai Youheng, a staff member of the Civil Training Section, received them and agreed to report and handle the matter after consulting with their superiors. They then went to the Garrison Headquarters and the Municipal Public Security Bureau to petition, submitting documents.

Went to Beijing Last Night

Seven general representatives of the National Private Postal Bureaus, including Hua Yunjin, Yin Yuantong, Wang Dashi, Zhuang Gengtang, Qiu Zhengsheng, Ren Shiting, and Pan Wentian, took the Beijing-Shanghai Express night train from Shanghai North Railway Station to Beijing at 11:00 PM last night to petition the Fifth Plenary Session, the National Government, the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive院, and the Ministry of Communications. Representatives along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, such as Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and Zhenjiang, boarded the train on the spot and went to Beijing at the same time. As for the representatives along the Yangtze River, they have already gone to Beijing one after another.

Gather for Petition

A letter from the general representatives of the National Private Postal Bureaus to various places stated: "Dear Sirs, The joint meeting on December 9th resolved the case of 'Sub-telegram and sub-letter to various ports to send representatives to Nanjing on the 14th of this month to jointly petition the central government with the general representatives.' I am very grateful. It is also decided to gather in the capital with representatives from various places this morning and petition various agencies separately."

To Raise Funds for Mongolian and Tibetan Primary Schools

According to him, Qinghai is located on the border and has a backward culture. In recent years, the central government has actively developed the Northwest and promoted education in the border areas. Although it has gradually progressed and changed its old appearance, the Tibetan ethnic group and the youth of various monasteries still have few opportunities to study. The National Government awarded the plaques "Teaching First and Nurturing Righteousness" and the Executive院 awarded the plaque "Promoting Culture" to show encouragement. All expenses in the school, which are required 600 yuan every day, are borne by the author. Last year, due to the sudden increase in students, the school building was added, and the expenses were huge and difficult to raise. So far, it has not been completed. After the start of school this term, there are a lot of textbooks and educational supplies needed. I sent someone to Shanghai to buy them, but they have not been bought because of the need for money. The fourth-grade students will graduate next spring. In order to facilitate further education, it is planned to expand the senior class to complete the fundamental basis of Mongolian and Tibetan education. Therefore, I discussed with Shi Qingyang, the Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, to find a way. Mr. Shi is very caring and believes that if no way is found

rescue, it will inevitably lead to the interruption of education, which is a pity, we must rely on the power of gathering small efforts, and collect the power of everyone to make it easy, so introduced by Mr. Shi, to celebrities in Beijing and Shanghai, and those who care about Mongolian and Tibetan education,

Fundraising separately, the money donated, in addition to purchasing books and educational supplies, and allocating a part of the subsidy to school building expenses, the remaining number is deposited in the provincial treasury bank to be used as the school's fund, so that the Guanghui Temple Primary School has a basis for regular expenses, and border education can be perfected day by day. In the future, developing the Northwest, relying on the power of religion, and uniting to protect the border can also slightly relieve the central government's worries about Xigu and avoid the sigh of being unable to reach the whip. Moreover, the hearts of the people in Qing land are extremely corrupt, and most do not like their children to study. There are 240 students in this school, which is not easy, but I hope to continue to work hard, break through the difficulties, so that everyone has the opportunity to be educated and not be used by foreigners. I will stay in Shanghai for a few more days, and after the public is over, I will return to Nanjing.

Long-Distance Telephone Calls on the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou Three Roads: Reduced Surcharges for Express Calls from New Year's Day

Charged at Twice the Rate of Ordinary Calls

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that long-distance telephone calls along the Beijing-Shanghai Highway, the Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway, and the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway are all sponsored by the Ministry of Communications. Express calls are usually charged three times more than ordinary telephone calls. In order to reduce the burden on the people, the Ministry of Communications has decided that from January 1 next year, all long-distance telephone calls on the Shanghai-Hangzhou, Beijing-Hangzhou, and Beijing-Shanghai three highways affiliated to the Ministry of Communications will be reduced to twice the rate of ordinary calls. (For example, the ordinary fare from Beijing to Shanghai is one yuan and five jiao, and the express fare is four yuan and five jiao each time, which will be reduced to three yuan.)

News of the Small Loan Office for Common People

Mr. Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and Mr. Zhao Dihua, Director of the Finance Department, concerned about the common people of this province and to help those who run small businesses, had a proposal to set up a small loan office. It was to be jointly operated by Jin Cheng, Farmers, and Jiangsu banks. Yesterday, a meeting was held at the Jin Cheng Bank in Shanghai, and Mr. Wu Yunzhai, Manager of Jin Cheng Bank in Shanghai, Mr. Hou Houpei, Deputy Manager of Farmers Bank, and Mr. Tian Shitai, Executive of Jiangsu Bank, were appointed as directors of the board. Yang Zhaoxiong and Chen Qixiang, commissioned by the Finance Department, were appointed as supervisors. The loan regulations and detailed rules of procedure were also approved, and Hou Houpei was elected as the executive director. The loan rules limit the use of funds to approximately four categories: (1) Purchasing goods or raw materials, (2) Purchasing craft and agricultural implements, (3) Promoting the sale of domestic goods with advance payments, and (4) Other productive uses. All small agricultural, industrial, and commercial operators with a fixed address and a legitimate business are eligible to apply for loans. The general office is located in Zhenjiang Farmers Bank, and the first sub-office is located in Jiangsu Bank outside Zhenjiang city. It will be established and start lending soon. The minimum loan is one yuan, and the maximum should not exceed two hundred yuan. In the future, the common people with small businesses will surely benefit greatly. It is said that the director and deputy director of the office have also been internally determined and will be announced soon.
